// Skies (for reference)
// 0XSKY101 Hub 1 - stars with blue and planet, etc. - 991010
// 0XSKY102 Hub 1 - stars with major blue stripe and asteroids
// 0XSKY103 Hub 1 - stars only - all black
// 0XSKY301 Hub 3 - green clouds
// 0XSKY302 Hub 3 - brown clouds
// 0XSKY303 Hub 3 - gray clouds
// 0XSKY400 Hub 4 - plain black sky for new planet (dae32)
// 0XSKY4B1 Hub 4 - Stars
// 0XSKY4B2 Hub 4 - Reversed stars - use with 0XSKY4B1 parallax

// === End of DAEDALUS MAPINFO ===
